&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Chihaktiimochilòo.

 ☞<a href="i2.htm#istittaɬammi">istittaɬammi</a>
<br><font size="+2"><b><a name="hasikanatli"></a>hasikanatli</b> </font>
<font size="+2">hour </font>
&nbsp; [/hasi /kanat-li]
 <i>Usage: </i>Variant occurs frequently in fast, casual speech.
 <i>Var: hasiyaaⁿli</i>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Hasikanatli istóklóffìinamon aati ombitìikaifan aɬɬalao.
 <i>A couple of hours from now I'm going to the funeral.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Himáaka tíkkìilit hasikanatlistóklóffìinamon.
 <i>A couple of hours from now.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Hasiyaaⁿlisnámpoosi?
 <i>What time is it?</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Hasikanatlisnámpoosi?
 <i>What time is it?</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Hasikanatlistóklo.
 <i>It's two o'clock.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Hasiyaaⁿlistóklo.
 <i>It's two o'clock.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Hasiyaaⁿlistóklon hókkìitat ɬóppotli.
 <i>It's two-thirty.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Hasikanatlischáffàako.
 <i>It's one o'clock.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Hasikanatlistáɬɬàapo.
 <i>It's five o'clock.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font size="0">(IB, VC)</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Hasikanatli istóklóffìinakon ilaliti.
 <i>I came a couple of hours ago.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font size="0">(IB)</font>

 ☞<a href="h.htm#hotihna">hotihna</a>
<br><font size="+2"><b><a name="hoɬka"></a>hoɬka</b> </font>
<font size="+2">sofkey </font>
&nbsp;<font color="#080000">Cul:  Popular traditional southeastern Indian dish made with corn. Corn is pounded in a large wooden mortar, culled and sifted repeatedly, boiled in water with lye (or baking soda) in a large three-footed iron pot over a wood fire. Generally served hot or cold traditionally without seasoning. It can be drunk or eaten with a spoon depending on the consistency, which can vary between a thin gruel to a watery porridge. The term `sofkey' comes from Creek.</font>&nbsp;
<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;<i><a href="h.htm#hoɬkachi">hoɬkachi</a></i>

<br><font size="+2"><b><a name="hopàaki pínha"></a>hopàaki pínha</b> </font>
<font size="+2">way far off</font>
&nbsp; [/hopàaki /pínha]
 ☞<a href="p.htm#pínha">pínha</a>
<br><font size="+2"><b><a name="hopáhki"></a>hopáhki</b> </font>
<font size="+2">a long distance, very far</font>
 [<i>hgr</i>]
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Hopáhkin wìikalihchi.
 <i>I live far away.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Hopáhkihchi.
 <i>It's too far.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Hopááⁿkihchi.
 <i>It's very far.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Hopáaⁿkìhchon aɬɬalao.
 <i>I'm going far away.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Hopáhkihchon achìita?
 <i>Do you live far?</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Ichóot ommiima ibi hopáhkitík ibìimok chinìilit albinafan stilachiifòokok sooplit, oaboslit, akkáamit ittanówwat nihtállo cháffàakahchóot ittanówwat ɬoyohkat ilachihchootoolo.
 <i>If it was a deer, even though they killed it far away, when they killed it, they carried it on their backs and when they got it to their camp, they skinned it and barbecued it, that's the way they would go and would usually be gone for a week and then they would turn around and go back.</i> <font size="0">(NHN)</font><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Akkáamiya maatabalàakat amaakat námpotík aati námpotík ittillokòolimok amaakáaⁿ hopahkin oɬachiifòokok tikba ostootifòokak akkat albiná hokatoolo.
 <i>That's what happened, they'd go and camp out, there would be several people, several of them would get together and they'd go a long way, and when they got there they would build a fire and that's what they'd call camp.</i> <font size="0">(NHN)</font><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Oklahomayok hopáako.
 <i>Oklahoma is a long ways.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Hopáhkin maawiiskachoⁿiska?
 <i>Are you calling long distance?/Are you way over there?</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
